"race_human_lore" "The Tau'ri were created by the Ancients, an ancient and incredibly advanced race, the products of the first evolution of humans, who wanted to populate the Milky Way with intelligent life forms. However, the project was not completed, as the Ancients had to leave the planet due to an outbreak of an epidemic. Through Some time ago, the Tau'ri planet was found by the High System Lord Ra, who seized control of the planet and, with the help of the Stargate, spread the human race to many other planets."

 "race_asgard_lore" "The Asgards are one of the most advanced modern alien civilizations. The Asgards treat humans favorably and sometimes share their advanced technology with them. Physiologically, the representatives of this race are the classic gray men familiar from science fiction." 
 "race_ori_lore" "The Ori are an aggressive religious faction of the Ancients who developed into an independent society after the flight of the Ancients from their home galaxy. One of the most highly developed civilizations in the four known galaxies. Used faith in themselves on other, lower beings to increase their power ."
